### 2021年度，股票简称为深赛格的公司的稀释每股收益是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To complete the SQLite SQL query to find the diluted earnings per share (EPS) for the company with the stock abbreviation "深赛格" in the year 2021, we need the following table:

- Income_Statement

This table contains the necessary financial information such as net profit, number of shares, and other relevant data to calculate the diluted earnings per share. 

Therefore, we will need to query the Income_Statement table to retrieve the data for the company with the stock abbreviation "深赛格" in the year 2021 and calculate the diluted earnings per share using the formula:

Diluted EPS = (Net Profit - Preferred Dividends) / (Weighted Average Number of Diluted Shares Outstanding)

Once we have the necessary data from the Income_Statement table, we can calculate the diluted earnings per share for the company with the stock abbreviation "深赛格" in the year 2021.

### 2021年度，股票简称为深赛格的公司的稀释每股收益是多少？
 SELECT
******
 稀释每股收益
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '深赛格';
Gold SQL: SELECT `稀释每股收益` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '深赛格' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2022年度，股票简称为万科A的公司的营业收入是多少？
 SELECT
******
营业收入 
 FROM Income_Statement 
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '万科A';
Gold SQL: SELECT `营业收入` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '万科A' AND `年度` = '2022'

### 2021年度，股票代码为32的公司的投资活动产生的现金流出小计是多少？
 SELECT
******
 投资活动产生的现金流出小计
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票代码 = 32;
Gold SQL: SELECT `投资活动产生的现金流出小计` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票代码` = '32' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2021年度，股票简称为深振业A的公司的归属少数股东的综合收益是多少？
 SELECT
******
 归属少数股东的综合收益
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '深振业A';
Gold SQL: SELECT `归属少数股东的综合收益` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '深振业A' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2021年度，股票代码为40的公司的筹资活动现金流入小计是多少？
 SELECT
******
 筹资活动现金流入小计 
 FROM 
 Cash_Flow_Statement 
 WHERE 
 年度 = '2021' AND 股票代码 = '40';
Gold SQL: SELECT `筹资活动现金流入小计` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票代码` = '40' AND `年度` = '2021'

The tables needed for the SQL query are:
1. Balance_Sheet

We will use the Balance_Sheet table to filter the data for the company with stock code 34 and retrieve the value of "资产：应收款项融资" for the specified date.

The SQL query will look something like this:
```sql
SELECT "资产：应收款项融资"
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票代码 = 34 AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31';
```

### 2021年度，股票代码为58的公司的取得借款收到的现金是多少？
 SELECT
******
 取得借款收到的现金
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票代码 = 58;

### 2021年度，股票简称为深物业A的公司的营业收入是多少？
 SELECT
******
 营业收入 
 FROM Income_Statement 
 WHERE 年度 = '2021' AND 股票简称 = '深物业A';
Gold SQL: SELECT `营业收入` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '深物业A' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2022年度，股票代码为8的公司的经营活动现金流入小计是多少？
 SELECT
******
 经营活动现金流入小计 
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement 
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票代码 = 8;
Gold SQL: SELECT `经营活动现金流入小计` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票代码` = '8' AND `年度` = '2022'

### 2022年度，股票代码为5的公司的分配股利、利润或偿付利息支付的现金是多少？
 SELECT
******
分配股利_利润_偿付利息支付的现金
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票代码 = 5;
Gold SQL: SELECT `分配股利、利润或偿付利息支付的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票代码` = '5' AND `年度` = '2022'

### 2021年度，股票简称为深康佳A的公司的筹资活动现金流入小计是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To complete the SQLite SQL query to find the total cash inflow from financing activities for the company with the stock abbreviation "深康佳A" in the year 2021, we need the following table:

- Cash_Flow_Statement

This table contains the cash flow information for the company, including details on cash inflows and outflows from various activities such as operating, investing, and financing activities. We can use this table to filter the data for the company with the stock abbreviation "深康佳A" and the year 2021 to calculate the total cash inflow from financing activities.

So, the SQL query will involve selecting and summing up the "筹资活动现金流入小计" column from the Cash_Flow_Statement table for the company with the stock abbreviation "深康佳A" in the year 2021.
******

### 2021年度，股票简称为深康佳A的公司的筹资活动现金流入小计是多少？
 SELECT
******
 筹资活动现金流入小计 
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement 
 WHERE 年度 = '2021' AND 股票简称 = '深康佳A';
Gold SQL: SELECT `筹资活动现金流入小计` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '深康佳A' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2021年度，股票简称为华控赛格的公司的信用减值损失是多少？
 SELECT
******
 信用减值损失
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2021
 AND 股票简称 = '华控赛格';
Gold SQL: SELECT `信用减值损失` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '华控赛格' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2021年度，股票简称为皇庭国际的公司的支付的各项税费是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To complete the SQLite SQL query to find out the amount of taxes paid by the company with the stock abbreviation "皇庭国际" in the year 2021, we need the "Income_Statement" table.

Here is the step-by-step SQL query:

1. Select the column "税金及附加" from the "Income_Statement" table.
2. Filter the rows where the "股票简称" is "皇庭国际" and the "年度" is 2021.
3. Sum up the values in the "税金及附加" column to get the total taxes paid by the company.

The SQL query will look like this:

```sql
SELECT SUM(税金及附加) AS Total_Taxes_Paid
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 股票简称 = '皇庭国际' AND 年度 = 2021;
```

This query will give you the total amount of taxes paid by the company with the stock abbreviation "皇庭国际" in the year 2021.

### 2021年度，股票简称为皇庭国际的公司的支付的各项税费是多少？
 SELECT
******
 税金及附加 
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = '2021' AND 股票简称 = '皇庭国际';
Gold SQL: SELECT `支付的各项税费` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '皇庭国际' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2022年度，股票代码为66的公司的偿还债务支付的现金是多少？
 SELECT
******
 偿还债务支付的现金
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022
 AND 股票代码 = 66;
Gold SQL: SELECT `偿还债务支付的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票代码` = '66' AND `年度` = '2022'

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为深中华A的公司的资产：其他非流动资产是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产：其他非流动资产 
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '深中华A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT `资产：其他非流动资产` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE `股票简称` = '深中华A' AND `截止日期` = '2021-12-31'

### 2022年度，股票代码为1的公司的支付的各项税费是多少？
 SELECT
******
税金及附加
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票代码 = 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT `支付的各项税费` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票代码` = '1' AND `年度` = '2022'

### 2022年度，股票简称为深纺织A的公司的综合收益总额是多少？
 SELECT
******
综合收益总额 
 FROM Income_Statement 
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '深纺织A';
Gold SQL: SELECT `综合收益总额` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '深纺织A' AND `年度` = '2022'

### 2021年度，股票代码为5的公司的营业外收入是多少？
 SELECT
******
营业外收入 
 FROM Income_Statement 
 WHERE 年度 = '2021' AND 股票代码 = '5';
Gold SQL: SELECT `营业外收入` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `股票代码` = '5' AND `年度` = '2021'

### 2022年度，股票简称为深物业A的公司的取得借款收到的现金是多少？
 SELECT
******
 取得借款收到的现金
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '深物业A';
Gold SQL: SELECT `取得借款收到的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `股票简称` = '深物业A' AND `年度` = '2022'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票代码为5的公司的资产：应收款项融资是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产：应收款项融资 
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票代码 = 5 AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT `资产：应收款项融资` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE `股票代码` = '5' AND `截止日期` = '2022-12-31'

#
### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为万科A的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 ROUND((SELECT SUM(负债合计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '万科A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31') / (SELECT SUM(资产总计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '万科A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'), 2) AS 资产负债率;
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '万科A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为深圳华强的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 ROUND((SELECT SUM(负债合计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31') / (SELECT SUM(资产总计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'), 2) AS 资产负债率;
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为美丽生态的公司的净资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债合计 / 所有者权益合计) AS 净资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '美丽生态' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '美丽生态' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为大悦城的公司的资产负债率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the asset-liability ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "大悦城" as of 2021-12-31, we need the Balance_Sheet table. 

The asset-liability ratio is calculated as follows:
Asset-Liability Ratio = Total Assets / Total Liabilities

Therefore, we need the following columns from the Balance_Sheet table:
- Total Assets (资产总计)
- Total Liabilities (负债合计)

We will use these columns to calculate the asset-liability ratio in the SQL query.

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为大悦城的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 ROUND((SELECT SUM(负债合计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '大悦城' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31') / (SELECT SUM(资产总计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '大悦城' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'), 2) AS 资产负债率;
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '大悦城' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

### 2021年度，股票简称为中洲控股的公司的成本收入比是多少？
 SELECT
******
营业成本 / 营业收入 as 成本收入比
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '中洲控股';
Gold SQL: SELECT 营业总成本 / 营业总收入 AS 成本收入比 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '中洲控股' AND 年度 = '2021'

### 2022年度，股票简称为京基智农的公司的成本收入比是多少？
 SELECT
******
营业成本 / 营业收入 as 成本收入比
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '京基智农';
Gold SQL: SELECT 营业总成本 / 营业总收入 AS 成本收入比 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '京基智农' AND 年度 = '2022'

### 2021年度，股票简称为平安银行的公司的成本收入比是多少？
 SELECT
******
 营业成本 / 营业收入 as 成本收入比
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '平安银行';
Gold SQL: SELECT 营业总成本 / 营业总收入 AS 成本收入比 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '平安银行' AND 年度 = '2021'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为中国长城的公司的资产负债率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the asset-liability ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "中国长城" as of December 31, 2022, we need the Balance_Sheet table. 

The asset-liability ratio is calculated as follows:
Asset-Liability Ratio = Total Assets / Total Liabilities

Therefore, we need the Total Assets and Total Liabilities values from the Balance_Sheet table for the company with the stock abbreviation "中国长城" as of December 31, 2022. 

We do not need the Cash_Flow_Statement or Income_Statement tables for this specific calculation.

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为中国长城的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 SUM(负债合计) / SUM(资产总计) AS 资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '中国长城' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '中国长城' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为深纺织A的公司的净资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债合计 / 所有者权益合计) AS 净资产负债率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '深纺织A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深纺织A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为泛海控股的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计,负债合计, (负债合计 / 资产总计) AS 资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '泛海控股' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '泛海控股' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'
------------------------------------------
30

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为深康佳A的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 负债合计 as 资产负债率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

### 2021年度，股票简称为神州高铁的公司的成本收入比是多少？
 SELECT
******
营业成本 / 营业收入 as 成本收入比
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '神州高铁';
Gold SQL: SELECT 营业总成本 / 营业总收入 AS 成本收入比 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '神州高铁' AND 年度 = '2021'

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为华控赛格的公司的净资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债合计 - 资产总计) / 资产总计 AS 净资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '华控赛格' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '华控赛格' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'
------------------------------------------

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为皇庭国际的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计,负债合计
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '皇庭国际'
AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '皇庭国际' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为华锦股份的公司的净资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债合计 / 所有者权益合计) AS 净资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '华锦股份' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '华锦股份' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为美丽生态的公司的净资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债合计 / 所有者权益合计) AS 净资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '美丽生态' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '美丽生态' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为深华发A的公司的净资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债合计 / (负债合计 + 所有者权益合计)) AS 净资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '深华发A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深华发A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

#
### 截止到2021-12-31，股票简称为东旭蓝天的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 ROUND((SELECT SUM(负债合计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31') / (SELECT SUM(资产总计) FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'), 2) AS 资产负债率;
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31'

### 2022年度，股票简称为深华发A的公司的成本收入比是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the cost income ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "深华发A" in the year 2022, we need the following tables:
1. Income_Statement table to get the total operating cost and total operating income for the company.
2. Balance_Sheet table to get the company's full name for reference.

We will use the Income_Statement table to calculate the cost income ratio using the formula:
Cost Income Ratio = Total Operating Cost / Total Operating Income

So, the SQL query will involve joining the Income_Statement table with the Balance_Sheet table on the stock code, filtering the data for the year 2022 and the stock abbreviation "深华发A", and then calculating the cost income ratio.

### 2022年度，股票简称为深华发A的公司的成本收入比是多少？
 SELECT
******
股票简称, 营业成本, 营业收入, 营业成本/营业收入 as 成本收入比
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '深华发A';
Gold SQL: SELECT 营业总成本 / 营业总收入 AS 成本收入比 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深华发A' AND 年度 = '2022'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为平安银行的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计, 负债合计, (负债合计*1.0/资产总计) AS 资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '平安银行' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '平安银行' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

To calculate the cost income ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "中洲控股" in the year 2022, we need the following tables:
1. Income_Statement table to get the total operating costs and operating income.
2. Cash_Flow_Statement table to get the net cash flow from operating activities.

We will use the data from these tables to calculate the cost income ratio for the company "中洲控股" in the year 2022.

### 2022年度，股票简称为中洲控股的公司的成本收入比是多少？
 SELECT
******
股票简称, 营业成本 / 营业收入 AS 成本收入比
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '中洲控股';
Gold SQL: SELECT 营业总成本 / 营业总收入 AS 成本收入比 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '中洲控股' AND 年度 = '2022'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为深纺织A的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 ROUND((SUM(负债合计) / SUM(资产总计)), 2) AS 资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '深纺织A' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深纺织A' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

The required tables for the SQLite SQL query are:
1. Balance_Sheet

We will use the Balance_Sheet table to retrieve the asset total for the company with the stock abbreviation "东旭蓝天" for the years 2021 and 2022. Then, we can calculate the asset total growth rate using the formula:

Asset Total Growth Rate = ((Asset Total for 2022 - Asset Total for 2021) / Asset Total for 2021) * 100

By using the data from the Balance_Sheet table, we can calculate the asset total growth rate for the company "东旭蓝天" as of 2022-12-31.

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为东旭蓝天的公司的资产总计同比增长率是多少？
 SELECT
******
((SELECT "资产总计" FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') - (SELECT "资产总计" FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / (SELECT "资产总计" FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31') * 100 AS "资产总计同比增长率" FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT ((SELECT `资产总计` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') - (SELECT `资产总计` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / (SELECT `资产总计` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '东旭蓝天' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31') AS 同比增长率

### 2022年度，股票简称为飞亚达的公司的成本收入比是多少？
 SELECT
******
 营业成本 / 营业收入 AS 成本收入比
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '飞亚达';
Gold SQL: SELECT 营业总成本 / 营业总收入 AS 成本收入比 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '飞亚达' AND 年度 = '2022'

### 2022年度股票简称为深深房A的公司的筹资活动现金流入小计同比增长率是多少？
 SELECT
******
((筹资活动现金流入小计 - (SELECT 筹资活动现金流入小计 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度=2021 AND 股票简称='深深房A')) / (SELECT 筹资活动现金流入小计 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度=2021 AND 股票简称='深深房A')) * 100 
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement 
 WHERE 年度=2022 AND 股票简称='深深房A';
Gold SQL: SELECT ((SELECT `筹资活动现金流入小计` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深深房A' AND 年度 = '2022') - (SELECT `筹资活动现金流入小计` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深深房A' AND 年度 = '2021')) / (SELECT `筹资活动现金流入小计` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深深房A' AND 年度 = '2021') AS 同比增长率
------------------------------------------
45

### 2022年度股票简称为德赛电池的公司的取得借款收到的现金同比增长率是多少？
 SELECT
******
((SELECT 取得借款收到的现金 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '德赛电池') - (SELECT 取得借款收到的现金 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '德赛电池')) / (SELECT 取得借款收到的现金 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '德赛电池') * 100 AS 同比增长率 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '德赛电池';
Gold SQL: SELECT ((SELECT `取得借款收到的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池' AND 年度 = '2022') - (SELECT `取得借款收到的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池' AND 年度 = '2021')) / (SELECT `取得借款收到的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池' AND 年度 = '2021') AS 同比增长率

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为国药一致的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 ROUND((SUM(负债合计) / SUM(资产总计)), 2) AS 资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为北方国际的公司的净资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债合计 / 所有者权益合计) AS 净资产负债率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '北方国际' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '北方国际' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为中集集团的公司的资产：应收票据净额同比增长率是多少？
 SELECT
******
((应收票据净额 - LAG(应收票据净额, 1) OVER (ORDER BY 截止日期)) / LAG(应收票据净额, 1) OVER (ORDER BY 截止日期)) * 100 as 应收票据净额同比增长率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '中集集团' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT ((SELECT `资产：应收票据净额` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '中集集团' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') - (SELECT `资产：应收票据净额` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '中集集团' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / (SELECT `资产：应收票据净额` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '中集集团' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31') AS 同比增长率

### 截止到2022-12-31，股票简称为华联控股的公司的资产负债率是多少？
 SELECT
******
 ROUND((SUM(负债合计) / SUM(资产总计)), 2) AS 资产负债率
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '华联控股' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31';
Gold SQL: SELECT 负债合计 / 资产总计 AS 资产负债率 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '华联控股' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'
------------------------------------------
50

#
### 2022年度，股票简称为神州数码的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / 资产总计 AS 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '神州数码';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '神州数码' AND 年度 = '2022') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '神州数码' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%') AS 净资产收益率

### 2021年度，股票简称为深华发A的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
股本, 股本 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深华发A' AND 截止日期 = '2021年度';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深华发A' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深华发A' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 总资产收益率

### 2021年度，股票简称为农产品的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
股票简称, (净利润 / 总资产) AS 总资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '农产品';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '农产品' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '农产品' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 总资产收益率
------------------------------------------
53

### 2022年度，股票简称为泛海控股的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债与所有者权益总计 / 资产总计) * 100
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '泛海控股'
 AND 年度 = 2022;
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '泛海控股' AND 年度 = '2022') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '泛海控股' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%') AS 总资产收益率

### 股票简称为深圳华强的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 流动资产合计 as 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率
------------------------------------------
55

******
To calculate the return on equity (ROE) for the company with the stock abbreviation "京基智农" in the year 2021, we need the Income_Statement table. 

The ROE formula is: Net Income / Total Equity

So, we need the Net Income and Total Equity values from the Income_Statement table for the company with the stock abbreviation "京基智农" in the year 2021. 

Therefore, we need the Income_Statement table to complete the SQLite SQL query.

### 2021年度，股票简称为京基智农的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / NULLIF(净资产, 0) as 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '京基智农';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '京基智农' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '京基智农' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 净资产收益率
------------------------------------------
56

### 股票简称为神州数码的公司的总资产周转率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "神州数码" (Shenzhou Digital), we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company.
2. Income_Statement table to get the total revenue for the company.

We will use the formula for total asset turnover ratio:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Total Revenue / Total Assets

Therefore, we need data from both the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables to calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "神州数码".

### 股票简称为神州数码的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 营业总收入 as 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '神州数码';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '神州数码' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '神州数码' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '神州数码' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率
------------------------------------------
57

#
### 2021年度，股票简称为泛海控股的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '泛海控股';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '泛海控股' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '泛海控股' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 净资产收益率

58

### 股票简称为南玻A的公司的总资产周转率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "南玻A" (assuming it is the same as the stock code), we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company with the stock abbreviation "南玻A".
2. Income_Statement table to get the net sales or total revenue for the company with the stock abbreviation "南玻A".

We will use the total asset turnover ratio formula:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Sales / Total Assets

So, we need data from both the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables to calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "南玻A".
******

******
Balance_Sheet | Income_Statement

### 股票简称为南玻A的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 营业总收入 as 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '南玻A';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '南玻A' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '南玻A' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '南玻A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率

### 2022年度，股票简称为沙河股份的公司的净资产收益率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the return on equity (ROE) for the company with the stock abbreviation "沙河股份" in the year 2022, we need the Income_Statement table. 

The ROE formula is: 
ROE = Net Income / Shareholders' Equity

In the Income_Statement table, we can find the necessary values for Net Income and Shareholders' Equity to calculate the ROE. 

So, we need the Income_Statement table to complete the SQLite SQL query for calculating the ROE for the company with the stock abbreviation "沙河股份" in the year 2022.

### 2022年度，股票简称为沙河股份的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / NULLIF(净资产, 0) as 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '沙河股份';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '沙河股份' AND 年度 = '2022') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '沙河股份' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%') AS 净资产收益率
------------------------------------------
60

### 2022年度，股票简称为华控赛格的公司的总资产收益率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company "华控赛格" in the year 2022, we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company in 2022.
2. Income_Statement table to get the net profit for the company in 2022.

We will use the formula for total asset turnover ratio:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Profit / Total Assets

So, we need to join the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables on the "股票代码" and "年度" columns to get the required data for the calculation.

### 2022年度，股票简称为华控赛格的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(Net_Income / Total_Assets) * 100 AS ROA
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.Stock_Code = Balance_Sheet.Stock_Code
WHERE Income_Statement.Year = 2022
AND Income_Statement.Stock_Name = '华控赛格';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '华控赛格' AND 年度 = '2022') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '华控赛格' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%') AS 总资产收益率

#
### 2022年度，股票简称为深赛格的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / 资产总计 as 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '深赛格';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深赛格' AND 年度 = '2022') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深赛格' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%') AS 净资产收益率
------------------------------------------
62

### 股票简称为飞亚达的公司的总资产周转率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "飞亚达" (Feiyada), we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company.
2. Income_Statement table to get the net sales or total revenue for the company.

We will use the formula for total asset turnover ratio:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Sales / Total Assets

So, we need to join the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables on the stock code and then calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "飞亚达".
******

******
Balance_Sheet | Income_Statement

### 股票简称为飞亚达的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 营业总收入 as 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '飞亚达';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '飞亚达' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '飞亚达' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '飞亚达' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率

#
### 2021年度，股票简称为德赛电池的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / 所有者权益合计 AS 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '德赛电池';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 净资产收益率

### 2021年度，股票简称为特力A的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(净利润 / 总资产) AS 总资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '特力A';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '特力A' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '特力A' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 总资产收益率
------------------------------------------

### 2022年度，股票简称为德赛电池的公司的总资产收益率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company "德赛电池" in the year 2022, we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company in 2022.
2. Income_Statement table to get the net profit for the company in 2022.

We will use the formula for total asset turnover ratio:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Profit / Total Assets

So, we need to join the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables on the "股票代码" and "年度" columns to calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company "德赛电池" in 2022.
******
Sure! Based on your response, provide only the required tables in the following format: 'Table_Name_1 | Table_Name_2' to simplify your response, which means using '|' to separate different tables. Don't use any other format or add any additional explanations.
******
Balance_Sheet | Income_Statement
******

### 2022年度，股票简称为德赛电池的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(负债与所有者权益总计 / 资产总计) * 100
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池'
 AND 年度 = 2022;
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池' AND 年度 = '2022') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '德赛电池' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%') AS 总资产收益率

### 2021年度，股票简称为ST 星源的公司的总资产收益率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "ST 星源" in the year 2021, we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company in 2021.
2. Income_Statement table to get the net income for the company in 2021.

We will use the formula for total asset turnover ratio:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Income / Total Assets

So, we need to join the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables on the stock code and year to get the necessary data for the calculation.

### 2021年度，股票简称为ST 星源的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(净利润 / 总资产) * 100 AS 总资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = 'ST 星源';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = 'ST 星源' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = 'ST 星源' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 总资产收益率

### 2021年度，股票简称为深南电A的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(Net_Income / Total_Assets) * 100 AS ROA
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE Income_Statement.年度 = 2021
AND Balance_Sheet.股票简称 = '深南电A';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深南电A' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深南电A' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 总资产收益率

So, we need the following tables to complete the SQLite SQL query:
1. Income_Statement
2. Balance_Sheet

We will use the Net Profit from the Income_Statement table and the Total Equity from the Balance_Sheet table to calculate the ROE for the company "国药一致" in the year 2021.

### 2021年度，股票简称为国药一致的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / 资产总计 AS 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '国药一致';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 净资产收益率

### 股票简称为深振业A的公司的总资产周转率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "深振业A", we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company.
2. Income_Statement table to get the net sales or revenue for the company.

We will use the formula for total asset turnover ratio:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Sales / Average Total Assets

So, we need to join the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables on the stock code to get the necessary data for the calculation.
******

******
Balance_Sheet | Income_Statement

### 股票简称为深振业A的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 营业总收入 as 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '深振业A';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深振业A' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深振业A' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深振业A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率
------------------------------------------
70

### 股票简称为深康佳A的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / NULLIF(流动资产合计 + 非流动资产合计, 0) AS 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率

### 2021年度，股票简称为方大集团的公司的净资产收益率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the return on equity (ROE) for the company with the stock abbreviation "方大集团" in the year 2021, we need the Income_Statement table. 

We will need the following columns from the Income_Statement table:
- 股票代码 (Stock Code)
- 股票简称 (Stock Abbreviation)
- 年度 (Year)
- 净利润 (Net Profit)
- 归属于母公司所有者的净利润 (Net Profit Attributable to Parent Company)

We will use the formula for ROE:
ROE = Net Profit / Shareholders' Equity

To calculate ROE, we need the Net Profit and Shareholders' Equity. Shareholders' Equity can be calculated as:
Shareholders' Equity = 净资产 = 归属于母公司所有者的净利润

Therefore, we will use the Income_Statement table to calculate the ROE for the company with the stock abbreviation "方大集团" in the year 2021.

### 2021年度，股票简称为方大集团的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / NULLIF(净资产, 0) as 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '方大集团';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '方大集团' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '方大集团' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 净资产收益率
------------------------------------------
72

### 2022年度，股票简称为深深房A的公司的净资产收益率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the return on equity (ROE) for the company with the stock abbreviation "深深房A" in the year 2022, we need the Income_Statement table. 

The ROE formula is: Net Income / Total Equity

So, we need the following columns from the Income_Statement table:
- 股票代码 (Stock Code)
- 股票简称 (Stock Abbreviation)
- 年度 (Year)
- 净利润 (Net Profit)
- 归属于母公司所有者的净利润 (Net Profit Attributable to Parent Company)
- 所有者权益总计 (Total Equity)

Therefore, the Income_Statement table is needed to complete the SQLite SQL query for calculating the ROE for the company with the stock abbreviation "深深房A" in the year 2022.

### 2022年度，股票简称为深深房A的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / NULLIF(净资产, 0) as 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 股票简称 = '深深房A';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深深房A' AND 年度 = '2022') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深深房A' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%') AS 净资产收益率

#
### 2021年度，股票简称为深康佳A的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / 资产总计 AS 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '深康佳A';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '深康佳A' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 净资产收益率

### 2021年度，股票简称为北方国际的公司的总资产收益率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "北方国际" in the year 2021, we need to use the Income_Statement and Balance_Sheet tables. 

We will need the following columns from each table:
- From the Balance_Sheet table: "股票简称" (Stock Abbreviation), "资产总计" (Total Assets)
- From the Income_Statement table: "股票简称" (Stock Abbreviation), "净利润" (Net Profit)

We will use the formula for total asset turnover ratio:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Profit / Total Assets

Therefore, the SQL query will involve joining the Income_Statement and Balance_Sheet tables on the "股票简称" column and calculating the total asset turnover ratio for the company with the stock abbreviation "北方国际" in the year 2021.

******
Balance_Sheet | Income_Statement

### 2021年度，股票简称为北方国际的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(Net_Income / Total_Assets) * 100 AS ROA
FROM Income_Statement
JOIN Balance_Sheet ON Income_Statement.股票代码 = Balance_Sheet.股票代码
WHERE Income_Statement.年度 = 2021
AND Balance_Sheet.股票简称 = '北方国际';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '北方国际' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '北方国际' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 总资产收益率
------------------------------------------

#
### 2021年度，股票简称为神州高铁的公司的总资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
(净利润 / 资产总计) * 100 AS 总资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 股票简称 = '神州高铁'
AND 年度 = 2021;
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '神州高铁' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '神州高铁' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 总资产收益率

### 2021年度，股票简称为华锦股份的公司的净资产收益率是多少？
 SELECT
******
净利润 / NULLIF(净资产, 0) as 净资产收益率
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 股票简称 = '华锦股份';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 净利润 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '华锦股份' AND 年度 = '2021') / (SELECT 所有者权益合计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '华锦股份' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%') AS 净资产收益率

1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company in 2022.

We will use the total assets from the Balance_Sheet table and the net profit from the Income_Statement table to calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company "美丽生态" in 2022.

### 股票简称为京基智农的公司的总资产周转率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company "京基智农", we need the following tables:
1. Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets for the company "京基智农".
2. Income_Statement table to get the net sales or revenue for the company "京基智农".

We will use the total asset turnover ratio formula:
Total Asset Turnover Ratio = Net Sales / Total Assets

So, we need to join the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables on the "股票代码" and "股票简称" columns to get the necessary data for the calculation.
******

******
Balance_Sheet | Income_Statement

### 股票简称为京基智农的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 营业总收入 as 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '京基智农';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '京基智农' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '京基智农' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '京基智农' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率
------------------------------------------
79

### 股票简称为国药一致的公司的总资产周转率是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To calculate the total asset turnover ratio for the company "国药一致" (Guo Yao Yi Zhi), we need to use the Balance_Sheet table to get the total assets and the Income_Statement table to get the total revenue.

So, we need the Balance_Sheet and Income_Statement tables to complete the SQLite SQL query.
******
Sure! Based on your response, provide only the required tables in the following format: 'Table_Name_1 | Table_Name_2' to simplify your response, which means using '|' to separate different tables. Don't use any other format or add any additional explanations.
******
Balance_Sheet | Income_Statement
******

### 股票简称为国药一致的公司的总资产周转率是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产总计 / 营业总收入 as 总资产周转率
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致';
Gold SQL: SELECT (SELECT 营业收入 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致' AND 年度 = '2022') / (((SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致' AND 截止日期 = '2022-12-31') + (SELECT 资产总计 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 股票简称 = '国药一致' AND 截止日期 = '2021-12-31')) / 2) AS 总资产周转率
------------------------------------------
80

### 2022年度，哪家公司在净利润上的值是最小的？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To complete the SQLite SQL query to find the company with the smallest net profit in 2022, we need the following table:

Income_Statement table, which contains the following columns:
- 股票代码 (Stock Code)
- 股票简称 (Stock Abbreviation)
- 年度 (Year)
- 净利润 (Net Profit)
- 公司全称 (Company Full Name)

We will use the Income_Statement table to filter the data for the year 2022 and then find the company with the smallest net profit value.

The SQL query will involve selecting the company with the smallest net profit in 2022 from the Income_Statement table.
******
Sure! Based on your response, provide only the required tables in the following format: 'Table_Name_1 | Table_Name_2' to simplify your response, which means using '|' to separate different tables. Don't use any other format or add any additional explanations.
******

### 2022年度，哪家公司在净利润上的值是最小的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022
 ORDER BY 净利润
 LIMIT 1;

### 截止到2022-12-31，哪家公司在所有者权益：盈余公积上的值是最大的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'
 ORDER BY 所有者权益：盈余公积 DESC
 LIMIT 1;

 SELECT
******
 公司全称

 WHERE 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'

 LIMIT 1;

### 截止到2022-12-31，哪家公司在所有者权益：未分配利润上的值是最小的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'
 ORDER BY 所有者权益：未分配利润
 LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT 公司全称 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 截止日期 = '2022-12-31' ORDER BY 所有者权益：未分配利润 ASC LIMIT 1

- Cash_Flow_Statement

### 2022年度，哪家公司在筹资活动现金流出小计上的值是最大的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称, 筹资活动现金流出小计 
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022
 ORDER BY 筹资活动现金流出小计 DESC
 LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT 公司全称 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度 = '2022' ORDER BY 筹资活动现金流出小计 DESC LIMIT 1

### 截止到2022-12-31，哪家公司在资产：递延所得税资产上的值是最小的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称
 FROM Balance_Sheet
 WHERE 截止日期 = '2022-12-31'
 ORDER BY 资产：递延所得税资产
 LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT 公司全称 FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE 截止日期 = '2022-12-31' ORDER BY 资产：递延所得税资产 ASC LIMIT 1

### 2022年度，哪家公司在综合收益总额上的值是最大的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022
 ORDER BY 综合收益总额 DESC
 LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT 公司全称 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 年度 = '2022' ORDER BY 综合收益总额 DESC LIMIT 1

### 2022年度，哪家公司在信用减值损失上的值是最大的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022
 ORDER BY 信用减值损失 DESC
 LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT 公司全称 FROM Income_Statement WHERE 年度 = '2022' ORDER BY 信用减值损失 DESC LIMIT 1

- Cash_Flow_Statement

We will use the Cash_Flow_Statement table to retrieve the values for "经营活动现金流入小计" for the year 2022 for all companies. Then, we can compare these values to find the company with the highest value.

The SQL query will involve selecting the company with the maximum value in the "经营活动现金流入小计" column for the year 2022.

### 2022年度，哪家公司在经营活动现金流入小计上的值是最大的？
 SELECT
******
公司全称
FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
WHERE 年度 = 2022
ORDER BY 经营活动现金流入小计 DESC
LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT 公司全称 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度 = '2022' ORDER BY 经营活动现金流入小计 DESC LIMIT 1

### 2022年度，哪家公司在支付给职工以及为职工支付的现金上的值是最小的？
 SELECT
******
 公司全称, 支付给职工以及为职工支付的现金
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022
 ORDER BY 支付给职工以及为职工支付的现金
 LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT 公司全称 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE 年度 = '2022' ORDER BY 支付给职工以及为职工支付的现金 ASC LIMIT 1

### 2021年深圳华侨城的投资活动产生的现金流量净额是多少？
 SELECT
******
投资活动产生的现金流量净额
FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
WHERE 公司全称 = '深圳华侨城'
AND 年度 = 2021;
Gold SQL: SELECT `投资活动产生的现金流量净额` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%深圳华侨城%' AND 年度 LIKE '%2021%'
------------------------------------------
91

### 2021年深圳市深粮控股的负债：一年内到期的非流动负债是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To complete the SQLite SQL query to find the "一年内到期的非流动负债" of Shenzhen Shenzhen Grain Holdings in 2021, we need the Balance_Sheet table.

The SQL query would be:
```sql
SELECT 股票代码, 股票简称, 截止日期, 负债：一年内到期的非流动负债
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 公司全称 = '深圳市深粮控股' AND 截止日期 = '2021年';
```

This query will retrieve the required information from the Balance_Sheet table for Shenzhen Shenzhen Grain Holdings in 2021.

### 2021年深圳市深粮控股的负债：一年内到期的非流动负债是多少？
 SELECT
******
一年内到期的非流动负债 
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 公司全称 = '深圳市深粮控股'
AND 截止日期 = '2021'
LIMIT 1;
Gold SQL: SELECT `负债：一年内到期的非流动负债` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%深圳市深粮控股%' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%'
------------------------------------------
92

### 2021年深圳能源集团的资产：无形资产净额是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产：无形资产净额
FROM Balance_Sheet
WHERE 公司全称 = '2021年深圳能源集团';
Gold SQL: SELECT `资产：无形资产净额` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%深圳能源集团%' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2021%'
------------------------------------------
93

### 2021年深圳华强实业的收到其他与筹资活动有关的现金是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To find the "收到其他与筹资活动有关的现金" for 深圳华强实业 in 2021, we need to look at the Cash_Flow_Statement table. 

So, the table needed to complete the SQLite SQL query is Cash_Flow_Statement. 

The SQL query to find the "收到其他与筹资活动有关的现金" for 深圳华强实业 in 2021 would be:

```sql
SELECT 收到其他与筹资活动有关的现金
FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳华强实业' AND 年度 = 2021;
```

### 2021年深圳国华网安科技的资产减值损失是多少？
 SELECT
******
资产减值损失
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = '2021' AND 公司全称 = '深圳国华网安科技';
Gold SQL: SELECT `资产减值损失` FROM Income_Statement WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%深圳国华网安科技%' AND 年度 LIKE '%2021%'
------------------------------------------
95

### 2021年深圳市振业的投资收益中：对联营企业和合营企业的投资收益是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To complete the SQLite SQL query to find the investment income of Shenzhen Zhenye in 2021 from associated and joint ventures, you will need the Income_Statement table.

Here is the SQL query you can use:

```sql
SELECT 投资收益中：对联营企业和合营企业的投资收益
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 年度 = '2021' AND 公司全称 = '深圳市振业';
```

This query will select the investment income from associated and joint ventures for Shenzhen Zhenye in the year 2021 from the Income_Statement table.

### 2021年国药集团一致药业的销售商品、提供劳务收到的现金是多少？
 SELECT
******
销售商品、提供劳务收到的现金 
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2021 AND 公司全称 = '国药集团一致药业';
Gold SQL: SELECT `销售商品、提供劳务收到的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%国药集团一致药业%' AND 年度 LIKE '%2021%'
------------------------------------------
97

### 2022年深圳市皇庭国际企业的所有者权益：资本公积：库存股是多少？
 SELECT
******
资本公积, 库存股
FROM Income_Statement
WHERE 公司全称 = '2022年深圳市皇庭国际企业';
Gold SQL: SELECT `所有者权益：资本公积：库存股` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%深圳市皇庭国际企业%' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%'

### 2021年深圳市全新好的收回投资收到的现金是多少？ Which tables do you need to complete the SQLite SQL query? Let's think step by step.
******
To complete the SQLite SQL query for finding the cash received from the investment recovery of Shenzhen Quanxin in 2021, you will need the Cash_Flow_Statement table. 

Here is the step-by-step process:
1. Identify the columns needed: You will need the columns "股票代码" (Stock Code), "股票简称" (Stock Abbreviation), "年度" (Year), and "收回投资收到的现金" (Cash received from investment recovery).

2. Write the SQL query:
```sql
SELECT 股票代码, 股票简称, 年度, 收回投资收到的现金
FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
WHERE 股票简称 = '深圳市全新好' AND 年度 = '2021';
```

This query will retrieve the cash received from the investment recovery for Shenzhen Quanxin in the year 2021 from the Cash_Flow_Statement table.
******
Sure! Based on your response, provide only the required tables in the following format: 'Table_Name_1 | Table_Name_2' to simplify your response, which means using '|' to separate different tables. Don't use any other format or add any additional explanations.
******
Cash_Flow_Statement

### 2021年深圳市全新好的收回投资收到的现金是多少？
 SELECT
******
收回投资收到的现金
 FROM Cash_Flow_Statement
 WHERE 公司全称 = '深圳市全新好'
 AND 年度 = 2021;
Gold SQL: SELECT `收回投资收到的现金` FROM Cash_Flow_Statement WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%深圳市全新好%' AND 年度 LIKE '%2021%'
------------------------------------------
99

### 2022年泛海控股的所有者权益：实收资本（或股本）是多少？
 SELECT
******
实收资本（或股本）
 FROM Income_Statement
 WHERE 年度 = 2022 AND 公司全称 = '泛海控股';
Gold SQL: SELECT `所有者权益：实收资本（或股本）` FROM Balance_Sheet WHERE `公司全称` LIKE '%泛海控股%' AND 截止日期 LIKE '%2022%'
